<p style="margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item 8.01
Other Events.</b></span></p>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-size: 10pt">Zion Oil and Gas, Inc., a Delaware corporation,
which has an active petroleum exploration operation onshore Israel on the Megiddo-Jezreel area,<span style="background-color: white">&#160;announces
the approval on December 6, 2023 of </span></span>its workplan by the Israel Ministry of Energy for its Megiddo-Jezreel #1 well (MJ-01)
recompletion project.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Amidst the war in Israel following the atrocities on October 7, Zion
has maintained secure operations with the site and rig unharmed. The company now targets a Q1 start date post-holidays. Zion has secured
service contractors and ancillary items required for efficient operations. This workplan approval follows the acquisition of Exploration
License 434 on September 19, 2023. This &#8220;Megiddo Valleys License&#8221; spans approximately 75,000 acres and signifies a deep commitment
to Israel&#8217;s energy landscape. Zion will be implement cutting-edge technologies and stimulation methods to potentially unlock previous
and newly identified zones of interest.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Item
9.01</b></span> <span style="font-size: 10pt"><b>Financial Statements and Exhibits.</b></span></p>


<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">(d) Exhibits</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><b>SIGNATURES</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE DATED DECEMBER 6, 2023

<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. Receives Regulatory Approval for Strategic
Recompletion Project in Israel</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Zion Oil &amp; Gas targets early 2024 to move forward with MJ-01
recompletion operations.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">DALLAS, Texas, and CAESAREA, Israel, December 6, 2023 /PRNewswire/
-- Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. (OTCQX: ZNOG) announces the approval of its workplan by the Israel Ministry of Energy for its MJ-01 recompletion
project.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;Israel is open for business and we are grateful for the Israeli
government&rsquo;s green light on our workplan, allowing us to move ahead with the MJ-01 recompletion project,&rdquo; said Rob Dunn, CEO of
Zion Oil &amp; Gas. &ldquo;This is an exciting time for Zion as we implement cutting-edge technologies and stimulation methods to potentially
unlock previous and newly identified zones of interest.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Amidst the war in Israel following the atrocities on October 7, Zion
has maintained secure operations with the site and rig unharmed. The company now targets a Q1 start date post-holidays. Zion has secured
service contractors and ancillary items required for efficient operations.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">This workplan approval follows the acquisition of Exploration License
434 on September 19. This &ldquo;Megiddo Valleys License&rdquo; spans approximately 75,000 acres and signifies a deep commitment to Israel&rsquo;s
energy landscape.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><IMG SRC="ex99-1_001.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;Our journey continues with an unwavering faith in God and the
ongoing support of our shareholders,&rdquo; said John Brown, Zion Founder and Chairman. &ldquo;We appreciate all the support from so many
who have joined us in this journey of faith for Israel&rsquo;s oil and gas.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Zion Oil &amp; Gas, a US public company traded on OTCQX Best Market,
explores for oil and gas onshore in Israel.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Zion currently has a Unit Program with Warrants until December 31,
inviting supporters to be part of Israel&rsquo;s promising energy future.</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Investments can be made directly via Zion&rsquo;s website at www.zionoil.com
(www.zionoil.com/dspp) through Zion&rsquo;s Direct Stock Purchase Program.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><I>&ldquo;The steadfast love of the Lord never
ceases; his mercies never come to an end; they are new every morning; great is your faithfulness.&rdquo;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Lamentations 3:22-23</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center"><I>&ldquo;And let us not grow weary of doing good,
for in due season we will reap, if we do not give up.&rdquo;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Galatians 6:9</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Contact:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Andrew Summey</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">VP, Marketing and Investor Relations</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Zion Oil &amp; Gas, Inc. (OTCQX: ZNOG)</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">12655 North Central Expressway, Suite 1000, Dallas, TX 75243</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Telephone: 888-891-9466</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Email: info@zionoil.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">www.zionoil.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: left; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS: Statements in this
communication that are not historical fact, including, but not limited to, statements regarding Zion&rsquo;s operations and the
results therefrom, including testing and completion; Zion&rsquo;s ability to discover and produce oil in commercial quantities;
Zion&rsquo;s ability to continue as a going concern; operational risks in ongoing exploration efforts; regulatory approvals needed
for exploration within our license and the rig&rsquo;s operation; the effect, if any, of the coronavirus pandemic on the timing of
the operation of the well; <FONT>the effect, if any, of the uncertainties associated with wars and
skirmishes between Israel and other organizations and/or countries,</FONT> and liquidity for shareholders on the OTC market are
forward-looking statements as defined in the &ldquo;Safe Harbor&rdquo; provisions of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of

uncertainties, and other unpredictable factors, many of which are described in Zion&rsquo;s periodic reports filed with the SEC and
are beyond Zion&rsquo;s control. These risks could cause Zion&rsquo;s actual performance to differ materially from the results
predicted by these forward-looking statements. These risks and uncertainties include, but are not limited to, those described in
Item 1A in Zion&rsquo;s Annual Report on Form 10-K, which is expressly incorporated herein by reference, and other factors as may
periodically be described in Zion&rsquo;s filings with the SEC. Zion can give no assurance that the expectations reflected in these
statements will prove to be correct and assumes no responsibility to update these statements.</P>
